                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>দুর্বল তড়িৎ বিশ্লেষ্য: <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-22-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>C</mi><msub><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>H</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>C</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>O</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>O</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>H</mi></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-285" style="width: 4.961em;                                         <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: কোষের emf তড়িৎদ্বারের ধাতুর (i) প্রকৃতি, (ii) দ্রবণে আয়নের ঘনমাত্রা ও (iii) দ্রবণের তাপমাত্রার ওপর নির্ভর করে।<br>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>সবল জারক + সবল বিজারক <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-31-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>&amp;#x2192;</mo></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-370" style="width: 1.027em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.822em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.395em, 1000.78em, 2.133em, -999.998em); top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-371"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-372" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">→</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.048em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.753em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo stretchy="false">→</mo></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-31">\rm \rightarrow</script></span> দুর্বল বিজারক + দুর্বল জারক&nbsp;<br>
এখানে সবল বিজারক Zn বিজারিত হয়ে দুর্বল জারক&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-32-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>Z</mi><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>n</mi><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mn>2</mn><mo>+</mo></mrow></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-373" style="width: 2.174em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.764em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.068em, 1001.76em, 2.133em, -999.998em); top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-374"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-375" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">Z</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-376"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.518em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.53em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-377" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">n</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.383em; left: 0.576em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-378"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-379"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-380" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-381" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">+</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.048em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.103em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">Z</mi><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">n</mi><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>2</mn><mo>+</mo></mrow></msup></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-32">\rm Zn^{2+}</script></span> এ পরিণত হয়েছে।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৫৮৩]</p>
</span>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>লবণ সেতুর বৈশিষ্ট্য:<br>
১. ক্যাটায়ন ও অ্যানায়নের বেগ সমান বা প্রায় সমান।<br>
২. ব্যবহৃত লবণ অ্যানোডে জারিত বা ক্যাথোডে বিজারিত হয় না।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৫৭৬]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>2F চার্জ দ্বারা সঞ্চিত Cu এর পরিমাণ = 63.5&nbsp;g<br>
<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-108-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2234;</mo></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1436" style="width: 0.658em; height: 2.215em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.148em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.753em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>∴</mo></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-108">\therefore</script></span>&nbsp;1F&nbsp;চার্জ দ্বারা সঞ্চিত Cu এর পরিমাণ = <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-109-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mfrac><mn>63.5</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>g</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>31.75</mn><mtext>&amp;#xA0;</mtext><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>g</mi></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1439" style="width: 6.559em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 5.371em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.027em, 1005.37em, 2.502em, -999.998em); top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1440"><span class="mfrac" id="MathJax-Span-1441"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.395em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; font-family: MathJax_Main;">63.5</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.33em, 4.141em, -999.998em); clip: rect(0.904em, 1001.39em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 1.395em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block;
